[PHASE-C] 951-001 | H2088 zeh | Reg 99 (kindness)
Term type: Property term — Hebrew demonstrative particle
DESC (confirmed): Term directs attention to inner-being quality, state, act, or object — identifying or intensifying inner-being engagement

AV-VERIFY 951-001 | Isa 58:6
AV: Isa 58:6 — "'Is not this the fast that I choose: to loose the bonds of wickedness, to undo the straps of the yoke, to let the oppressed go free, and to break every yoke?'"
DESC covers: Directing attention to an inner-being act — zeh ("this") points to the genuine inner fast God chooses: justice, liberation, solidarity.
VERSE also shows: The zeh identifies the true fasting as justice-action. The inner dimension is the orientation of the fast — not bodily deprivation for its own sake, but the inner commitment to righteousness that liberates the oppressed. The particle points precisely to this inner-characterised act.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE

AV-VERIFY 951-001 | Isa 66:2
AV: Isa 66:2 — "All these things my hand has made, and so all these things came to be, declares the Lord. But this is the one to whom I will look: he who is humble and contrite in spirit and trembles at my word."
DESC covers: Directing attention to an inner-being quality — zeh ("this is the one") points to humility, contrition, and trembling as the inner characteristics God looks for.
VERSE also shows: The three qualities — humble, contrite in spirit, trembles at the word — are precisely inner-being qualities named by zeh as the object of divine attention. God looks to the person whose inner character matches this profile. The particle points with great precision to the inner-being content.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT — Isa 66:2 is an exceptionally rich anchor for a property term; the zeh identifies the inner-character profile with theological precision.
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Cognition
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: NONE
NOTES: The particle zeh functions as an inner-being identifier — it points to and specifies the object of divine attention or the act of inner recognition. The inner-being characteristic the particle frames across both anchors is: (Isa 58:6) the inner-oriented fast of justice, and (Isa 66:2) the inner character of humility and contrition. Both are about recognising and naming what is genuinely inner before God. With 17 verses the corpus spans many such identification moments. The underlying inner-being characteristic is cognitive identification and discernment — zeh as the vehicle of inner-being recognition. Cognition (the inner act of seeing, identifying, discerning what is truly inner) is the appropriate dimension. The UNCLASSIFIED label corrected to Cognition. DOMINANT-SUBJECT: NONE — the particle spans both divine and human perspectives.
PATCH-TARGET: wa_dimension_index.id = 7668

[PHASE-C] 952-001 | H5978 im.ma.di | Reg 99 (kindness)
Term type: Property term — "with me" marking divine presence as the condition
DESC (confirmed): Term frames divine presence as the condition of inner trust, security, and confident orientation toward God

AV-VERIFY 952-001 | Gen 28:20
AV: Gen 28:20 — "Then Jacob made a vow, saying, 'If God will be with me and will keep me in this way that I go, and will give me bread to eat and clothing to wear.'"
DESC covers: Divine presence as the condition of inner trust — "if God will be with me" frames the whole vow.
VERSE also shows: Jacob's conditional vow reveals the inner orientation: he is bargaining from a position of need and uncertainty. The "with me" is the condition upon which he will make God his God. The inner state is one of provisional trust — trust contingent on experienced presence.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE

AV-VERIFY 952-001 | Psa 23:4
AV: Psa 23:4 — "Even though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, I will fear no evil, for you are with me; your rod and your staff, they comfort me."
DESC covers: Divine presence as the condition of inner security — "you are with me" grounds the fearlessness directly.
VERSE also shows: The "with me" (im.ma.di) is the pivot of the verse — it is what transforms the valley of death from terror to security. The inner state is courage and comfort grounded entirely in divine presence. This is the paradigmatic expression of creaturely trust in divine accompaniment.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Dependence / Creatureliness
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: HUMAN
NOTES: Divine presence as the condition of the human creature's inner trust and security — the person's inner orientation is entirely dependent on divine accompaniment. Automated label Dependence/Creatureliness confirmed. Psa 23:4 is a paradigmatic anchor for this dimension.
PATCH-TARGET: wa_dimension_index.id = 7685

[PHASE-C] 952-002 | H5978 im.ma.di | Reg 99 (kindness)
Term type: Property term
DESC (confirmed): Term marks the zone of direct divine encounter with the self — whether affliction or care — as shaping the person's inner state

AV-VERIFY 952-002 | Job 6:4
AV: Job 6:4 — "For the arrows of the Almighty are in me; my spirit drinks their poison; the terrors of God are arrayed against me."
DESC covers: Divine encounter shaping the inner state — God's arrows are "in me"; my spirit drinks the poison.
VERSE also shows: The divine-human encounter here is afflictive — the im.ma.di zone is one of assault. The spirit internalises the divine arrows as poison. The inner state is one of spiritual devastation from divine encounter experienced as hostile.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE

AV-VERIFY 952-002 | Job 9:35
AV: Job 9:35 — "Then I would speak without fear of him, for I am not so in myself."
DESC covers: The zone of divine encounter shaping inner state — "I am not so in myself" reveals the inner condition away from the pressure of divine presence.
VERSE also shows: The "in myself" (be.nap.shi) describes Job's inner condition apart from God's overwhelming presence — he knows he could speak freely without fear if God were not so terrifyingly present. The im.ma.di zone is what makes fearless speech impossible. The inner state is one of self-diminishment before divine presence.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Emotion — Negative
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: HUMAN
NOTES: The inner state of spiritual devastation and self-diminishment in the zone of direct divine encounter experienced as afflictive. The automated label Divine-Human Correspondence is present but these verses do not show mirroring — they show the human inner person overwhelmed by divine action. Correcting to Emotion — Negative: the inner states (spiritual poisoning, fearful self-diminishment) are negative emotional conditions shaped by the encounter.

[PHASE-C] 953-001 | H0120G a.dam | Reg 99 (kindness)
Term type: Property term — generic human term as bearer of inner moral condition

AV-VERIFY 953-001 | Gen 6:5
AV: Gen 6:5 — "The Lord saw that the wickedness of man was great in the earth, and that every intention of the thoughts of his heart was only evil continually."
DESC covers: Inner moral condition — "every intention of the thoughts of his heart was only evil continually" is the paradigmatic statement of the evil inclination.
VERSE also shows: The comprehensiveness is total: every intention, of the thoughts, of the heart, only evil, continually. The inner-being content is the saturation of the human heart by evil orientation. This is the darkest picture of the human moral condition in the Hebrew Bible.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE

AV-VERIFY 953-001 | Jer 17:5
AV: Jer 17:5 — "Thus says the Lord: 'Cursed is the man who trusts in man and makes flesh his strength, whose heart turns away from the Lord.'"
DESC covers: Inner moral condition — heart turning away from God; making flesh the ground of trust.
VERSE also shows: The inner moral failure is redirected trust — the heart turns from God toward human strength. The curse follows from the inner orientation. The contrast (implied: blessed is the one who trusts in God) frames the inner moral choice.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Moral Character
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: HUMAN

[PHASE-C] 953-002 | H0120G a.dam | Reg 99 (kindness)
Term type: Property term
DESC (confirmed): Human frailty and dependence before God — inner limitation and creaturely orientation defining adam

AV-VERIFY 953-002 | Isa 2:11
AV: Isa 2:11 — "The haughty looks of man shall be brought low, and the lofty pride of men shall be humbled, and the Lord alone will be exalted in that day."
DESC covers: Human frailty and dependence — pride brought low and humbled names the creaturely orientation that pride refuses; the exaltation of God alone names the proper inner recognition of creaturely limit.
VERSE also shows: The eschatological humbling reveals what the inner person must ultimately be — not self-exalting but creature before Creator. The pride of adam is precisely the refusal of creaturely dependence; its humbling is the restoration of the proper orientation.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE

AV-VERIFY 953-002 | Jer 10:23
AV: Jer 10:23 — "I know, O Lord, that the way of man is not in himself, that it is not in man who walks to direct his steps."
DESC covers: Inner limitation and creaturely orientation — "the way of man is not in himself" is the paradigmatic statement of creaturely dependence.
VERSE also shows: Jeremiah's confession is absolute — the human creature cannot determine its own way. This is the positive statement of Dependence/Creatureliness: the creature's inner orientation is rightly one of acknowledged limitation and reliance on God's direction.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Dependence / Creatureliness
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: HUMAN

[PHASE-C] 953-003 | H0120G a.dam | Reg 99 (kindness)
Term type: Property term
DESC (confirmed): Humanity as object of God's purposeful action — created in God's image, known, called to reflect divine character

AV-VERIFY 953-003 | Gen 1:26
AV: Gen 1:26 — "Then God said, 'Let us make man in our image, after our likeness. And let them have dominion over the fish of the sea and over the birds of the heavens.'"
DESC covers: Humanity as object of God's purposeful action — created in God's image and called to reflect divine character through dominion.
VERSE also shows: The image (tselem) and likeness (demut) ground humanity in a correspondence relationship with God. The dominion mandate flows from this inner-being constitution. The group describes what humanity is by divine design — a constitutive inner-being reality.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE

AV-VERIFY 953-003 | Mic 6:8
AV: Mic 6:8 — "He has told you, O man, what is good; and what does the Lord require of you but to do justice, and to love kindness, and to walk humbly with your God?"
DESC covers: Called to reflect divine character — the requirements (justice, kindness, humility) define the inner character humanity is called to embody.
VERSE also shows: The three requirements name inner dispositions: justice (moral orientation), kindness (relational orientation), humble walking (creaturely orientation). Together they sketch the inner-being profile of the person living in accordance with the divine image. A.dam is addressed as the one who can and must embody this.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Divine-Human Correspondence
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: HUMAN
NOTES: Humanity constituted in the divine image, called to reflect divine character — this is precisely Divine-Human Correspondence: the inner-being of the human person is defined by structural correspondence with God (image/likeness) and by the requirement to embody the character qualities that reflect God (justice, kindness, humility). The automated label Volition misses the constitutive correspondence structure; it is not primarily an act of will but an inner-being constitution. Correcting to Divine-Human Correspondence. DOMINANT-SUBJECT: HUMAN — it is the human person who bears the image and is addressed by the requirements.
PATCH-TARGET: wa_dimension_index.id = 7665

VERSE also shows: Moses is identified by this single inner quality — meekness. The superlative ("more than all people") marks it as the paradigmatic expression of this quality in the human person. The verse uses a.dam (earthly humanity) as the comparative set.

VERSE also shows: Meekness and poverty are paired — inner meekness and outer poverty together describe the person oriented toward God in humility and dependence. The fresh joy they obtain is itself an inner state. The a.dam reference frames this as a human-condition observation.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Moral Character
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: HUMAN

[PHASE-C] 954-001 | G5543 chrēstos | Reg 99 (kindness)
Term type: Characteristic term — adjective naming the quality
DESC (confirmed): Goodness/kindness as inner quality of God or persons — disposition of gracious favour expressed toward others

AV-VERIFY 954-001 | Rom 2:4
AV: Rom 2:4 — "Or do you presume on the riches of his kindness and forbearance and patience, not knowing that God's kindness is meant to lead you to repentance?"
DESC covers: Kindness as inner quality — God's kindness (chrēstotēs) is here presupposed by Paul; chrēstos (kind) is its adjectival form. The purpose of divine kindness is inner transformation (leading to repentance).
VERSE also shows: God's kindness has a telos — it is not merely favour but an inner-being invitation to change. The presumption upon it is itself an inner-being failure. The kindness is purposive, relational, and transforming.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE

AV-VERIFY 954-001 | Eph 4:32
AV: Eph 4:32 — "Be kind to one another, tenderhearted, forgiving one another, as God in Christ forgave you."
DESC covers: Disposition of gracious favour expressed toward others — "be kind to one another" names the human inner disposition; the grounding in divine action ("as God in Christ forgave you") frames it as a correspondence.
VERSE also shows: The three virtues — kind, tenderhearted, forgiving — are presented as inseparable inner qualities to be cultivated. The grounding in divine action (God's forgiveness) establishes that the human disposition mirrors the divine. The chrēstos quality is both a character virtue and a correspondence with God's own character.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Relational Disposition
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: NONE
NOTES: Goodness/kindness as the inner quality of gracious favour toward others — a relational disposition in both God (Rom 2:4) and the human person (Eph 4:32). The group spans both divine and human subjects across the 6-verse corpus. Dominant-subject NONE — genuinely dual. Automated label Moral Character is close but misses the relational orientation quality; the chrēstos virtue is fundamentally directed toward another. Correcting to Relational Disposition.
PATCH-TARGET: wa_dimension_index.id = 7662

[SESSION-D] DIM-103-SD003
REGISTRY: 103 (love)
SESSION-TARGET: D
DESCRIPTION: The dod groups in Reg 103 (533-001, 1602-001, 545-001) together span the full range of the beloved-love vocabulary: from the Songs human mutual delight to covenantal God-Israel love to intimate address. Session D should examine whether the dod/beloved vocabulary encodes a structural homology: the same inner-being quality of intense, exclusive, covenantal devotion manifests at both the divine-human covenantal level and the human interpersonal level. If confirmed across the full corpus, this would show that the love vocabulary of Scripture treats both divine and human love as expressions of the same inner-being characteristic — not mere analogy.

[PHASE-C] 535-001 | H3033 ye.di.dut | Reg 103 (love)
Term type: Characteristic term
DESC (confirmed): Term names Israel as the beloved of Gods soul — the most intimate inner designation, whose abandonment into enemy hands marks Gods deepest grief

AV-VERIFY 535-001 | Jer 12:7
AV: Jer 12:7 — I have forsaken my house; I have abandoned my heritage; I have given the beloved of my soul into the hands of her enemies.
DESC covers: Israel as the beloved of Gods soul — beloved of my soul is the most intimate divine designation; the abandonment marks deepest grief. The triple statement traces divine grief in the act of judgment. VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT | FLAG: NONE

[SESSION-B] DIM-103-002
REGISTRY: 103 (love)
DESCRIPTION: Group 535-001 (ye.di.dut — beloved of Gods soul, Reg 103) is anchored by Jer 12:7: I have given the beloved of my soul into the hands of her enemies. The phrase ye.di.dut nap.shi (beloved of my soul/nephesh) attributes an intimate inner-being category to God — God has a nephesh, and the beloved relationship is located there. This raises a significant inner-being question for Session B of Reg 103: does the love vocabulary of Reg 103 contain a sub-pattern of terms that attribute inner-being states to God with the same vocabulary used for human inner-being states? The terms ye.di.dut (beloved of my soul), ra.cha.mim (my heart yearns — Jer 31:20 in group 551-001), and the dod vocabulary (God as lover/beloved in Song and prophets) may all encode a divine inner-being reality using the same vocabulary as the human inner person. Session B should investigate whether Reg 103 contains a theological claim about divine inner-being experience, and how this connects to the programmes governing question about the inner characteristics of the human person.
PATCH-TARGET: wa_session_b_findings insert

DIMENSION: Relational Disposition
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: GOD
NOTES: Gods most intimate attachment — the beloved of my soul. Automated label Emotion-Negative corrected — the grief is the consequence; the characteristic is the relational bond. Correcting to Relational Disposition, GOD.
PATCH-TARGET: wa_dimension_index.id = 7781

[PHASE-C] 3158-001 | G3629 oiktirmon | Reg 111 (mercy)
Term type: Characteristic term — adjective naming compassionate character
DESC (confirmed): Term names compassion as the inner character of God and the standard for human inner disposition — to be merciful as God is merciful

AV-VERIFY 3158-001 | Luk 6:36
AV: Luk 6:36 — Be merciful, even as your Father is merciful.
DESC covers: Compassion as the standard — the divine compassion is the pattern for the human inner disposition.
VERSE also shows: The command is grounded in correspondence — be merciful AS your Father is merciful. The human inner character is called to mirror the divine. The Father's compassion is both the model and the motivation.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE

AV-VERIFY 3158-001 | Jam 5:11
AV: Jam 5:11 — you have seen the purpose of the Lord, how the Lord is compassionate and merciful.
DESC covers: Compassion as the inner character of God — oiktirmon (compassionate) and polusplagchnos (very merciful) as divine attributes.
VERSE also shows: Both terms name the inner character of God as the ground of the suffering believer's hope. The purpose of the Lord revealed in Job's story is that God's inner character is compassion and mercy.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Moral Character
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: NONE
NOTES: Compassion as the defining inner character quality — in God (Jam 5:11) and as the standard for the human person (Luk 6:36). The automated label Relational Disposition captures the toward-another quality but the dominant characteristic in both anchors is the inner character of the person (what God IS, what the human is called to BE). Correcting to Moral Character. DOMINANT-SUBJECT: NONE — both divine and human subjects are explicitly anchored across the 2-verse corpus.

[PHASE-C] 3169-001 | H3722A kip.per | Reg 111 (mercy)
Term type: Characteristic term — the priestly atoning act
DESC (confirmed): Term names the priestly/ritual act by which human guilt is covered before God and forgiveness granted — atonement as the mechanism addressing the persons moral condition

AV-VERIFY 3169-001 | Lev 4:20
AV: Lev 4:20 — the priest shall make atonement for them, and they shall be forgiven.
DESC covers: The priestly atoning act as the mechanism producing forgiveness — the sequence is atonement (priestly act) → forgiveness (divine response).
VERSE also shows: The forgiveness is the divine outcome of the priestly act. The inner-being content is the condition being addressed (guilt) and the result (restored standing before God). The mechanism is ritual but the effect is inner-being restoration.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE

AV-VERIFY 3169-001 | Lev 17:11
AV: Lev 17:11 — the blood that makes atonement by the life.
DESC covers: The mechanism of atonement — blood as the atoning agent, life for life as the substitutionary logic.
VERSE also shows: The inner-being content is the principle: life covers life. The moral accountability for life (guilt) is addressed by life given. The entire Levitical atonement system rests on this principle.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Dependence / Creatureliness
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: HUMAN
NOTES: The priestly atoning act that addresses human guilt before God — the creature's condition of moral accountability before the Creator addressed through the atonement mechanism. Automated label Moral Character is partial (it names the moral condition addressed) but misses the constitutive dimension: the atonement system reveals and addresses the creature's fundamental condition of guilt-before-God, which is Dependence/Creatureliness in its most acute form. The human person is entirely dependent on the divinely provided mechanism for the resolution of their moral condition. Correcting to Dependence/Creatureliness.
PATCH-TARGET: wa_dimension_index.id = 7836

[PHASE-C] 3176-001 | G2433 hilaskomai | Reg 111 (mercy)

[SESSION-D] DIM-111-SD001
REGISTRY: 111 (mercy)
SESSION-TARGET: D
DESCRIPTION: Reg 111 (mercy) contains a structural polarity that parallels but differs from the forgiveness polarity in Reg 64. Here the polarity is: the mercy seat (982-001 — the physical locus of divine-human meeting in mercy) at one end, and No Mercy (986-001 — the prophetic name embodying withdrawn mercy) at the other. Between these poles, the registry maps the full range of the mercy-atonement complex: divine compassion, priestly atonement, propitiatory cries, supplication, and human mercy. Session D should examine whether this polarity — the mercy seat as the locus of mercy granted, and No Mercy as the embodiment of mercy withdrawn — encodes the fundamental structure of the divine-human relationship as mercy-constituted: the human person stands before God at the mercy seat or faces the No Mercy verdict. No neutral ground exists. This may connect to the forgiveness polarity in Reg 64 (absolute forgiveness vs. permanent non-forgiveness) as a structural feature of C17 more broadly.
PATCH-TARGET: wa_session_research_flags insert

PATCH-TARGET: wa_dimension_index.id = 7849

---

AV: Heb 9:5 — Above it were the cherubim of glory overshadowing the mercy seat.
DESC covers: The mercy seat as the physical reality that Christ fulfils — the architectural context within which the fulfilment is understood.
VERSE also shows: Hebrews 9:5 names the mercy seat in its Levitical context (above the ark, overshadowed by the cherubim) precisely to establish the typological relationship — the physical mercy seat is the foreshadowing of Christ as the living hilasterios.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Divine-Human Correspondence
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: NONE
NOTES: The mercy seat fulfilled in Christ — the structural locus of divine-human encounter in mercy, now a person rather than a place, received by faith rather than blood-sprinkling. Divine-Human Correspondence is confirmed: the hilasterios is the constitutive point at which the divine and human meet in the mercy that defines the relationship. Automated label Relational Disposition corrected to Divine-Human Correspondence — this is not merely a relational orientation but a structural correspondence between the OT mercy seat and Christ, between divine initiative and human faith. DOMINANT-SUBJECT: NONE — both divine (God put forward) and human (received by faith) poles are constitutive.
PATCH-TARGET: wa_dimension_index.id = 7829

[PHASE-C] 992-001 | G3628 oiktirmos | Reg 111 (mercy)
Term type: Characteristic term — compassions as divine attribute
DESC (confirmed): Term names the compassions of God as his defining inner character — the mercies that motivate holy living and compassionate hearts as the inner garment of the new humanity

AV-VERIFY 992-001 | 2Cor 1:3
AV: 2Cor 1:3 — Blessed be the God and Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, the Father of mercies and God of all comfort.
DESC covers: Gods compassions as his defining inner character — Father of mercies (oiktirmon pater) as the defining divine title.
VERSE also shows: The Father of mercies is the source of all comfort — the divine compassion is not static but actively producing comfort in the lives of those who suffer. The inner-being content is the divine mercies as the origin of all human experience of consolation.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE

AV-VERIFY 992-001 | Col 3:12
AV: Col 3:12 — Put on then, as Gods chosen ones, holy and beloved, compassionate hearts, kindness, humility, meekness, and patience.
DESC covers: Compassionate hearts as the inner garment of the new humanity — oiktirmos (splanchna oiktirmou, hearts of compassion) as the first virtue to be put on.
VERSE also shows: The putting on of compassionate hearts grounds the character transformation in the divine mercies — the new humanity is clothed in the same compassion that characterises the Father of mercies. The inner-being content is the correspondence between divine mercies and human compassionate hearts.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Relational Disposition
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: NONE
NOTES: Gods compassions as defining inner character (2Cor 1:3) and the human putting on of compassionate hearts (Col 3:12) — both anchors present a relational disposition oriented toward others. The group spans divine (Father of mercies) and human (put on compassionate hearts) subjects. Automated label Relational Disposition confirmed. DOMINANT-SUBJECT: NONE — dual across the corpus.

[PHASE-C] 993-001 | G0448 anileos | Reg 111 (mercy)
Term type: Characteristic term — mercilessness
DESC (confirmed): Term names mercilessness as the inner orientation that forfeits mercy — and mercy as the disposition that triumphs over judgment

AV-VERIFY 993-001 | Jam 2:13
AV: Jam 2:13 — For judgment is without mercy to one who has shown no mercy. Mercy triumphs over judgment.
DESC covers: Mercilessness as the inner orientation that forfeits mercy — the one who has shown no mercy receives judgment without mercy.
VERSE also shows: The logic is a precise inner-being grammar: the inner orientation of mercilessness produces a corresponding judicial result. Conversely, mercy triumphs over judgment — the inner orientation of mercy reverses the judicial outcome. The inner-being characteristic is the orientation of the person (merciful or merciless) and its judicial consequence.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Moral Character
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: HUMAN
NOTES: Mercilessness as the inner moral orientation that forfeits mercy — a stable character disposition and its judicial consequence. Automated label Relational Disposition misses the character-quality dimension: anileos names what the person IS (merciless), with the judicial consequence flowing from that inner character. Correcting to Moral Character.

## Phase C — Dimension Discernment: Reg 130 (reconciliation)

Phase C for Reg 130 — 2 groups. This completes Phase C for all of C17.

Pointer sequences: Reg 130 Session B = DIM-130-001; Session D = DIM-130-SD001.

---

[PHASE-C] 1093-001 | G2643 katallagē | Reg 130 (reconciliation)
Term type: Characteristic term — reconciliation as the named state
DESC (confirmed): Term names reconciliation as the inner-relational restoration of broken relationship between God and humanity — the ending of enmity and establishment of peace at the relational core of personhood

AV-VERIFY 1093-001 | 2Cor 5:18
AV: 2Cor 5:18 — All this is from God, who through Christ reconciled us to himself and gave us the ministry of reconciliation.
DESC covers: Reconciliation as the restoration of broken relationship — God through Christ restoring the relationship between himself and humanity. The inner-being content is the ending of enmity and the establishment of peace at the relational core.
VERSE also shows: The reconciliation is entirely from God — divine initiative without human contribution. The resulting ministry of reconciliation places the reconciled person in the role of extending the same restoration to others. The inner-being content is both received (reconciliation) and expressed (ministry).
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Divine-Human Correspondence
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: GOD
NOTES: Reconciliation as the constitutive restoration of the divine-human relationship — the ending of enmity and establishment of peace at the relational core of personhood. The katallagē is precisely Divine-Human Correspondence: it names the structural reality of the restored relationship between God and humanity, not merely God's unilateral act toward a passive recipient, but the reconstitution of the relationship itself. Automated label Divine-Human Correspondence (KEYWORD_STRONG) confirmed. GOD is dominant — the reconciliation originates entirely in divine initiative.

[SESSION-D] DIM-130-SD001
REGISTRY: 130 (reconciliation)
SESSION-TARGET: D
DESCRIPTION: Reg 130 (reconciliation) contains only two groups (katallagē and katallassō), both anchored in the NT and both carrying Divine-Human Correspondence. Their small corpus (4 and 5 verses respectively) is concentrated in key Pauline reconciliation texts (2Cor 5, Rom 5, Col 1). Session D should examine whether the reconciliation vocabulary of Reg 130 functions as the structural summary of the entire C17 cluster: if C17 is about the relational-covenantal affections of the inner person, reconciliation (Reg 130) names the foundational inner-being state that makes all other C17 relational dispositions possible. The hypothesis: reconciliation is to C17 what covenant (Reg 34) is to its institutional structure — the inner-relational ground that constitutes the human person before God as a relational subject capable of love, mercy, forgiveness, peace, and fellowship. This would place Reg 130 at the apex of the C17 cluster despite being its smallest registry.
PATCH-TARGET: wa_session_research_flags insert

PATCH-TARGET: wa_dimension_index.id = 8165

---

[PHASE-C] 6114-001 | G2644 katallassō | Reg 130 (reconciliation)
Term type: Characteristic term — the act of reconciling
DESC (confirmed): Term names the act of reconciliation — the active work of restoring broken inner-relational standing, whether between God and humanity or within human relationships

AV-VERIFY 6114-001 | Rom 5:10
AV: Rom 5:10 — For if while we were enemies we were reconciled to God by the death of his Son, much more, now that we are reconciled, shall we be saved by his life.
DESC covers: The act of reconciliation — enemies reconciled to God by the death of the Son.
VERSE also shows: The reconciliation is explicitly from a state of enmity — the inner-being change is from enemy to reconciled person. The before (enemies) and after (reconciled) name the inner-being transformation at the relational core. The two tenses (were reconciled; are reconciled) span both the objective act and the ongoing state.
VERDICT: FULL ALIGNMENT
FLAG: NONE
ACTION: None

DIMENSION: Divine-Human Correspondence
DOMINANT-SUBJECT: GOD
NOTES: The act of reconciling broken inner-relational standing — the restoration of the divine-human relationship from enmity to peace. Automated label Divine-Human Correspondence (KEYWORD_STRONG) confirmed. GOD is dominant — the reconciling is from God's side; humanity receives the reconciliation.

Cross-registry patterns established across all of C17:
  1. Divine-Human Correspondence discipline: The programme has established a consistent distinction — D-HC requires structural mirroring of both poles; unilateral divine acts = Relational Disposition (GOD). Systematically corrected across all 9 registries.
  2. Relational Disposition vs. Moral Character: Love/mercy/compassion/peace as orientation toward another = RD; as stable character quality of the person = MC. Consistently applied from Reg 103 through Reg 117.
  3. Dependence/Creatureliness as the Reg 111 signature: The atonement-prayer-supplication vocabulary of mercy reveals that Reg 111 is constitutively about the creature's condition before God.
  4. Moral Character dominance in Reg 117: Silence/stillness/quiet vocabulary names cultivated inner character dispositions, not primarily emotional states.
  5. Structural polarity in Reg 64 and Reg 111: Both registries contain explicit limit-definitions (absolute forgiveness vs. permanent non-forgiveness; mercy seat vs. No Mercy). No other registries have analogous structural polarities.
  6. Reconciliation (Reg 130) as potential structural apex of C17.
